	color2 = { 255 255 255 }

	holy_order = yes

	culture = frankish

	primary = yes
	# Extra income due to banking, etc
	monthly_income = 10 # (Must be an integer between 1 and 512)
	title = GRANDMASTER
	foa = GRANDMASTER_FOA
}
